 The Disha Bill is a game-changer to ensure justice in crimes against women
 kuch ullekhneey praavdhaan is prakaar hai:1
 It amends the Indian Penal Code and the POCSO Act to provide for maximum punishment of capital punishment in rape, gang rape, child rape, acid-attack offenses
 2
 It ensures that the Criminal Procedure Code (CRPC) ensures that police investigations into rape and acid attack cases are completed in 7 days, further stating that judicial trial is completed within 14 days
 3
 This further CRPC ensures that all appeals and amendment petitions are disposed of within 3 months
 4
 It provides for setting up special sessions courts (fast-track courts) in every district to deal specifically with the crimes of rape, molestation and acid attack
 5
 The government has also announced the appointment of women government lawyers and special police teams to investigate these crimes
